## 利用矩检测量子同质性及其干涉实现

**Original Title:** Detection of quantum imaginarity using moments and its interferometric realization

**Authors:** Sudip Chakrabarty, Saheli Mukherjee, Ananda G. Maity, Bivas Mallick

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00164v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.00164v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-31


### 摘要

复数是量子理论公式所固有的，在实现广泛的量子信息处理任务的优势方面发挥着关键作用。尽管它们具有根本重要性，但用于检测量子同质性的实用和可扩展标准仍然相对未充分研究，特别是能够以减少实验费用来识别量子同质性的方法。在这项工作中，我们提出了一种现实且实验上可行的方法来使用基于动量的方法来检测量子相似性。我们的框架依赖于柯克伍德-狄拉克准概率分布的实验可访问时刻，能够在多体和多维系统中进行可扩展的检测，而无需全状态断层扫描。然后我们给出一个说明性的例子来支持我们的检测方案。最后，我们提出了一种测量这些时刻的干涉测量方案，为我们的检测协议的实验实施铺平了道路。


### Abstract

Complex numbers, intrinsic to the formulation of quantum theory, play a pivotal role in enabling advantages across a broad range of quantum information-processing tasks. Despite their fundamental importance, practical and scalable criteria for detecting quantum imaginarity remain relatively underexplored, particularly methods that enable its identification with reduced experimental overhead. In this work, we propose a realistic and experimentally feasible method to detect quantum imaginarity using moment-based approach. Our framework relies on experimentally accessible moments of the Kirkwood-Dirac quasiprobability distribution, enabling scalable detection in many-body and high-dimensional systems without requiring full state tomography. We then present an illustrative example to support our detection scheme. Finally, we present an interferometric scheme for measuring these moments, paving the way for experimental implementation of our detection protocol.

## 查询学习近泡利钻石距离中的稀疏个位数

**Original Title:** Query Learning Nearly Pauli Sparse Unitaries in Diamond Distance

**Authors:** Zahra Honjani, Mohsen Heidari

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00203v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.00203v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-31


### 摘要

我们研究学习近$（s，e）$-稀疏么元的问题，这意味着泡利谱集中在最多$s$分量上，Pauli $\ell_1 $-norm中剩余质量最多$。这门课概括了研究得很好的族，包括稀疏的么元、量子$k$-juntas、$2 ' k $-泡利维通道，以及深度$O（\log\log n）$电路与近Clifford电路的组合。   假设查询访问未知的几乎稀疏的单位$U$，我们的目标是有效地（在时间和查询复杂性方面）构建一个钻石距离接近$U$的量子通道。我们设计了一个学习算法，使用$\tilde{O}（s#6/e #4）$将查询转发到$U$，以及相关参数中的运行时间多项来实现这一保证。   一个关键贡献是一种高效的量子算法，在查询访问任意未知的正$U$的情况下，该算法估计幅度超过给定阈值$$的所有泡利系数（直到共享的全局相），从而将现有的稀疏恢复技术扩展到一般的正元。   我们还研究了具有有界Pauli $\ell_1 $-模的更广泛的么正类。对于该类，我们证明了指数查询下界$Q（2^{n/2}）$。我们引入了一个更宽松的准确性指标，即限制于一组输入状态的钻石距离。然后，我们证明，在这个度量下，Pauli $\ell_1 $-模一致由$L_1$有界的元元可以用$\tilde{O}（L_1 ' 8/e ' s ' s ' s）$学习。


### Abstract

We study the problem of learning nearly $(s,ε)$-sparse unitaries, meaning that the Pauli spectrum is concentrated on at most $s$ components with at most $ε$ residual mass in Pauli $\ell_1$-norm. This class generalizes well-studied families, including sparse unitaries, quantum $k$-juntas, $2^k$-Pauli dimensional channels, and compositions of depth $O(\log\log n)$ circuits with near-Clifford circuits.
  Given query access to an unknown nearly sparse unitary $U$, our goal is to efficiently (both in time and query complexity) construct a quantum channel that is close in diamond distance to $U$. We design a learning algorithm achieving this guarantee using $\tilde{O}(s^6/ε^4)$ forward queries to $U$, and running time polynomial in relevant parameters.
  A key contribution is an efficient quantum algorithm that, given query access to an arbitrary unknown unitary $U$, estimates all Pauli coefficients (up to a shared global phase) whose magnitude exceeds a given threshold $θ$, extending existing sparse recovery techniques to general unitaries.
  We also study the broader class of unitaries with bounded Pauli $\ell_1$-norm. For that class, we prove an exponential query lower bound $Ω(2^{n/2})$. We introduce a more relaxed accuracy metric which is the diamond distance restricted to a set of input states. Then, we show that, under this metric, unitaries with Pauli $\ell_1$-norm uniformly bounded by $L_1$ are learnable with $\tilde{O}(L_1^8/ε^{16})$.


---


## 用于超导器件中通用连续变量计算的构建模块

**Original Title:** Building Block For Universal Continuous Variables Computation In Superconducting Devices

**Authors:** Bruno A. Veloso, Ciro M. Diniz, Luiz O. R. Solak, Antonio S. M. de Castro, Daniel Z. Rossatto, Celso J. Villas-Bôas

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00212v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.00212v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-31


### 摘要

连续变量（CV）量子计算通过利用玻色子模的无限维Hilbert空间提供了基于量子位的计算的替代方案。尽管最近取得了进展，但高温平台尚未展示出能够进行通用计算的可扩展架构。在这里，我们设计并数值模拟了一种双层高温体系结构，该体系在实验可访问的区域内实现通用CV门组的所有五种相互作用（旋转、位移、压缩、克尔和分束器）。为此，我们使用DC-SQUID作为玻色子模，使用fluxium量子位来调解非线性相互作用，以及两个辅助量子位来实现高斯和多模式操作。通过调整通量和频率，我们在最先进的参数范围内的所有门上实现了高灵敏度（$\geq 98\%$）。该设计的模块化性质允许直接扩展，建立了一条可行的途径，实现基于超导电路的高保真、通用CV量子计算。


### Abstract

Continuous variable (CV) quantum computation offers an alternative to qubit-based computing by exploiting the infinite-dimensional Hilbert space of bosonic modes. Despite recent progress, superconducting platforms have yet to demonstrate a scalable architecture capable of universal computation.Here, we design and numerically simulate a two-layer superconducting architecture that implements all five interactions of the universal CV gate set (rotation, displacement, squeezing, Kerr, and beam splitter) within experimentally accessible regimes. To this end, we employ a DC-SQUID as the bosonic mode, a fluxonium qubit to mediate nonlinear interactions, and two ancillary qubits that enable Gaussian and multi-mode operations. By tuning fluxes and frequencies, we achieve high fidelities ($\geq 98\%$) across all gates within state-of-the-art parameter ranges. The modular nature of the design allows straightforward scaling, establishing a feasible pathway toward high-fidelity, universal CV quantum computation based on superconducting circuits.

## 晶体禁能光电流中的无场掩蔽量子几何

**Original Title:** Field-unmasked quantum geometry in a symmetry-forbidden photocurrent

**Authors:** Bumseop Kim, Aaron M. Burger, Zhenbang Dai, Sayed Ali Akbar Ghorashi, Adam Abirou, Md Al Helal, Vladmir M. Fridkin, Jonathan E. Spanier, Andrew M. Rappe

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00221v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.00221v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-31


### 摘要

频率和偏振分辨的光电流提供了一个敏感的探针隐藏的对称性和量子材料中的能带几何形状。在这里，我们研究了手性立方硅线石的全球晶体对称性禁止纵向奇在B磁光电流的Voigt几何。然而，我们观察到一个明显的纵向响应在整个可见光范围内，主要是线性的磁场，持续低于带隙，并表现出很强的螺旋度选择性，与圆形通道超过线性和反转符号时切换光螺旋度。我们解决了这个明显的矛盾，确定缺陷启用，场选择的自旋排序的机制，降低了有效的磁对称性，而不改变全球的晶体结构。第一性原理计算表明，O空位在邻近的Bi-O单元上产生带间隙束缚态和定域磁力，并由强SOC稳定。尽管与空位相关的空位配置保持能量简并并保持零场下的宏观T对称性，施加的磁场选择时间逆转-缺陷系综的扇形被破坏，并降低了子组的有效磁对称性，使B不变，从而解除了纵向选择规则。重要的是，这种场选择的对称性简化不仅仅是激活名义上禁止的光电流：它揭示了电子结构中编码的潜在量子几何响应。动量分辨计算表明，占主导地位的圆形和线性磁光流通道分别与布里渊区的富贝里弯曲区域和富量子度量区域在空间上相关。我们的结果建立了场选择缺陷对称性降低作为揭示隐藏的量子几何形状和激活手征量子材料中禁止的非线性光电流的途径。


### Abstract

Frequency- and polarization-resolved photocurrents provide a sensitive probe of hidden symmetry and band geometry in quantum materials. Here we study a chiral cubic sillenite whose global crystal symmetry forbids a longitudinal odd-in-B magneto-photocurrent in the Voigt geometry. Nevertheless, we observe a pronounced longitudinal response across the visible range that is predominantly linear in magnetic field, persists below the band gap, and exhibits strong helicity selectivity, with the circular channel exceeding the linear one and reversing sign upon switching light helicity. We resolve this apparent contradiction by identifying defect-enabled, field-selected spin ordering as the mechanism that lowers the effective magnetic symmetry without altering the global crystal structure. First-principles calculations show that O vacancies generate in-gap bound states and localized magnetic moments on neighboring Bi-O units, stabilized by strong SOC. Although symmetry-related vacancy configurations remain energetically degenerate and preserve the macroscopic T symmetry at zero field, an applied magnetic field selects a time-reversal-broken sector of the defect ensemble and reduces the effective magnetic symmetry to the subgroup that leaves B invariant, thereby lifting the longitudinal selection rule. Importantly, this field-selected symmetry reduction does more than activate a nominally forbidden photocurrent: it unmasks latent quantum-geometric responses encoded in the electronic structure. Momentum-resolved calculations show that the dominant circular and linear magneto-photocurrent channels spatially correlate with Berry-curvature-rich and quantum-metric-rich regions of the Brillouin zone, respectively. Our results establish field-selected defect symmetry lowering as a route to revealing hidden quantum geometry and activating forbidden nonlinear photocurrents in chiral quantum materials.


---


## 用于量子密钥分发系统的基于PGA的时间数字转换器的安全意识非线性研究

**Original Title:** A Security-Aware Nonlinearity Study of FPGA-Based Time-to-Digital Converters for Quantum Key Distribution Systems

**Authors:** Kun Qin, Carsten Trinitis

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00229v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.00229v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-31


### 摘要

基于PGA的时间数字转换器（TBC）中固有的非线性通常被视为校准问题，并主要通过后修正指标进行评估。然而，在量子密钥分发（QKD）中，原始延迟线不均匀性可能会影响符合时间，从而影响意外符合率和量子误比特率（QBER）。本文使用结合了随机定时不确定性和确定性非线性的保守系统级模型，分析了测量到的FPGA-PDC非线性如何传播到QKD定时指标。我们还提出了基于LU辅助延迟整形和放置约束的结构级缓解策略，以在无需统计校准的情况下减少严重的仓宽不规则性。该方法通过复制在低成本Zynq-7000现场可用的两个开源IDT来评估。与非优化设计相比，我们观察到积分非线性（INL）降低了14%-21%，导致QBER贡献降低，估计的秘密分数提高了3.7%-14.2%。这些结果表明，原始的FPGA-PDC非线性值得在时间敏感的QKD实现中明确考虑。


### Abstract

Intrinsic nonlinearity in FPGA-based time-to-digital converters (TDCs) is often treated as a calibration issue and evaluated mainly through post-correction metrics. In quantum key distribution (QKD), however, raw delay-line nonuniformity can affect coincidence timing and thereby influence accidental-coincidence rate and Quantum Bit Error Rate (QBER). This paper analyzes how measured FPGA-TDC nonlinearity propagates to QKD timing metrics using a conservative system-level model that combines random timing uncertainty and deterministic nonlinearity. We also propose fabric-level mitigation strategies based on LUT-assisted delay shaping and placement constraints to reduce severe bin-width irregularities without statistical calibrations. The method is evaluated by reproducing two open-source TDCs implemented on a low-cost Zynq-7000 FPGA. We observe reductions of 14\%-21\% in integral nonlinearity (INL) compared with the non-optimized design, leading to a reduced QBER contribution and an improvement by 3.7\%-14.2\% in the estimated secret fraction. These results suggest that raw FPGA-TDC nonlinearity deserves explicit consideration in timing-sensitive QKD implementations.


---


## 100年的旋转：基础物理学、暗物质、奇异的相互作用等等

**Original Title:** 100 years of spin: fundamental physics, dark matter, exotic interactions, and all that

**Authors:** Dmitry Budker, Tim Chupp, Klaus Kirch, W. Mike Snow

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00231v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.00231v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-31


### 摘要

一个世纪以来，旋转一直是对自然基本定律不可或缺的探索。文章反思了旋转在塑造现代物理学中的作用，从量子力学的早期到标准模型的最新精度测试。本文探讨了磁和电DMZ在测试CP和CPD对称性中的重要性，以及对奇异的依赖于旋转的相互作用的持续研究，这些相互作用可能揭示暗物质的本质及其与时空几何的联系。通过这些小插曲，我们表明旋转继续为当今物理学中最深刻的问题提供新的视角。


### Abstract

For a century, spin has been an indispensable probe of the fundamental laws of nature. A reflection on the role of spin in shaping modern physics is presented, from the early days of quantum mechanics to the latest precision tests of the Standard Model. The significance of magnetic and electric dipole moments in testing CP and CPT symmetries is surveyed, along with the ongoing searches for exotic spin-dependent interactions that may reveal the nature of dark matter and its connection to spacetime geometry. Through these vignettes, it is shown that spin continues to provide a fresh perspective on the most profound questions in physics today.


---


## 直接可视化量子点分子的能量结构

**Original Title:** Directly visualizing the energy level structure of quantum dot molecules

**Authors:** Heun Mo Yoo, Tanner M. Janda, Connor Nasseraddin, Jason R. Petta

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00232v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.00232v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-31


### 摘要

硅量子点的轨道、旋转和谷自由度支持许多旋转量子位操作模式。然而，在大参数空间范围内获得有关能量级谱的信息通常具有挑战性。我们展示了一种光谱学形式，它能够将双量子点的能量结构映射为水平失调、点间隧道耦合和磁场的函数。在单电子区域中，随着点间隧道耦合的增加，我们直接观察到从孤立量子点的类原子能量级到类分子成键和反成键状态的转变。我们还解决了磁场中地磁场和激发谷态的塞曼分裂。在双电子状态中，我们可以获得与失调相关的单重三重态分裂。我们的工作可能会扩展到更广泛的系统类别，例如强旋转轨道材料或接近量子点，从而允许直接提取各种能间隙。


### Abstract

The orbital, spin and valley degrees of freedom in silicon quantum dots support many modes of spin qubit operation. However, it is generally challenging to obtain information about the energy level spectrum over large ranges of parameter space. We demonstrate a form of spectroscopy that is capable of mapping the energy level structure of a double quantum dot as a function of level detuning, interdot tunnel coupling, and magnetic field. In the one electron regime, we directly observe the transition from the atom like energy levels of isolated quantum dots to molecular like bonding and anti bonding states with increasing interdot tunnel coupling. We also resolve the Zeeman splitting of ground and excited valley states in a magnetic field. In the two electron regime, we gain access to the detuning dependent singlet triplet splitting. Our work may be extended to a broader class of systems, such as strong spin-orbit materials or proximitized quantum dots, allowing the direct extraction of various energy gaps.


---


## 基于QFT的多输入并行加法器的量子非模乘

**Original Title:** Quantum Non-Moduler Multiplication with QFT-Based Multi Input Parallelized Adder

**Authors:** Murat Kurtand Selçuk Çakmak, Azmi Gençten

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00272v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.00272v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-31


### 摘要

在这项研究中，我们提出了一种基于QFT辅助并行加法方案的高效量子相乘方法。相乘阶段使用完全由Toffoli门组成的结构来实现，Toffoli门生成部分积。在第二阶段，使用基于QFT的加法器来累积这些部分结果。与传统的基于QFT的算术电路不同，所提出的设计消除了在中间相加过程中重复应用QFT和逆QFT（MQFT）操作。这导致总门数和电路复杂性显着减少，从而实现更资源高效的实施。为了证明所提出方法的可行性，设计了一个执行两个3比特数相乘的量子电路。该电路使用IBM量子模拟器进行测试和验证。结果表明，所提出的方法在门成本和电路深度方面提供了传统量子相乘技术更有效的替代方案。


### Abstract

In this study, we propose an efficient quantum multiplication approach based on a QFT-assisted parallelized addition scheme. The multiplication stage is implemented using a structure composed entirely of Toffoli gates, which generate partial products. In the second stage, these partial results are accumulated using a QFT-based adder. Unlike conventional QFT-based arithmetic circuits, the proposed design eliminates the repeated application of QFT and inverse QFT (IQFT) operations during intermediate summation processes. This leads to a significant reduction in the total gate count and circuit complexity, enabling a more resource-efficient implementation. To demonstrate the feasibility of the proposed approach, a quantum circuit that performs the multiplication of two 3-bit numbers is designed. The circuit is tested and validated using IBM quantum simulators. The results indicate that the proposed method provides a more efficient alternative to traditional quantum multiplication techniques in terms of gate cost and circuit depth.

## 关于测量、超决定论、自由意志和背景性

**Original Title:** On measurement, superdeterminism, free will, and contextuality

**Authors:** Mordecai Waegell

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00311v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.00311v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-31


### 摘要

超决定论最近受到了关注，作为对贝尔定理实验测试中出现的纠缠相关性进行局部因果解释的可能途径。虽然“超决定论”一词是贝尔创造的，指对实验者自由意志的限制，但直到最近才对其进行严格的定义。它现在已被定义为任何物理理论的一个属性，它会产生系统性地违反统计独立性。在这里，我们重点关注正式化非超确定性对物理理论的要求，并设定一个必须满足的标准，然后我们才能得出给定理论不是超确定性的结论。我们首先仔细研究物理理论如何决定我们在实体状态和响应函数方面进行测量时观察到的结果，以及超确定性和非超确定性理论之间的差异，以及我们在实验中使用的经过审查的随机抽样程序的行为。核心结果是，单个样本和测量结果必须代表观察到的分布，这将详细解释。这也有一个如何测量设置的代理人选择的影响，无论是自由或随机，我们认为，这个标准最终定义了什么自由/独立的实际意义。然后，我们讨论语境，并表明，在大多数情况下，超决定论是上下文。最后，我们讨论了具有不同实体状态和响应函数概念的不同物理理论如何产生相同的经验数据，以及相同的操作上下文如何以不同的形式出现。


### Abstract

Superdeterminism has received recent attention as a possible path toward a locally causal explanation of the entanglement correlations that appear in experimental tests of Bell's theorem. While the term `superdeterminism' was coined by Bell to refer to restrictions on the free will of experimenters, it was not rigorously defined until recently. It has now been defined as a property of any physical theory that produces systematic violations of statistical independence. Here we focus on formalizing the requirements that being nonsuperdeterministic places on a physical theory, and setting a standard that must be met before we can conclude that a given theory is not superdeterministic. We begin by carefully examining how a physical theory determines what outcomes we observe when performing measurements in terms of ontic states and response functions, and how this differs between superdeterministic and nonsuperdeterministic theories, in terms of the behavior of the types of vetted random sampling procedures that we use in experiments. The core result is that individual samples and measurement outcomes must be representative of the observed distributions, which is explained in detail. This also has a bearing on how measurement settings are chosen by agents, whether freely or randomly, and we argue that this standard ultimately defines what freedom/independence actually mean. We then discuss contextuality, and show that in most cases, superdeterminism is contextual. Finally, we discuss how different physical theories, with different notions of ontic states and response functions, can give rise to the same empirical data, and how the same operational contextuality may appear in different forms.


---


## 连续监测下无选择后量子多体动力学中异常等待时间分布

**Original Title:** Anomalous waiting-time distributions in postselection-free quantum many-body dynamics under continuous monitoring

**Authors:** Kazuki Yamamoto, Ryusuke Hamazaki

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00358v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.00358v1

**Submitted:** 2026-04-01


### 摘要

我们研究了连续监控的量子多体系统中量子跳跃的等待时间分布（WTD），其无条件动力学导致平凡的无限温度状态。我们证明，半链子系统的WTD表现出异常尾部，明显偏离了Poissonian分布，与整个系统的WTD形成鲜明对比。通过分析超操作符$\mathscr L_0$（通过从全刘维尔中去除与半链子系统相关的跳跃项来定义）的谱性质，我们发现半链WTD异常尾部的长期行为由具有最大实部的特征值$决定。我们进一步揭示了作为测量强度的函数的系统大小依赖性的质的变化：对于足够弱的测量，$X_0 $与系统大小成比例地减少，而对于强的测量，$X_0 $独立于系统大小而缩放，这表明异常半链WTD在热力学极限下的持续存在。WTD仅从量子跃迁的时空记录中提取，并且可以在没有后选择的情况下通过实验获得。我们的工作建立了一个光谱框架，了解非平凡的WTD子系统的监测量子动力学，并提供了一种新的诊断评估多体效应WTD。


### Abstract

We investigate waiting-time distributions (WTDs) of quantum jumps in continuously monitored quantum many-body systems, whose unconditional dynamics lead to the trivial infinite-temperature state. We demonstrate that the WTD of a half-chain subsystem exhibits an anomalous tail, markedly deviating from the Poissonian distribution in stark contrast to that of the whole system. By analyzing the spectral properties of the superoperator $\mathscr L_0$, which is defined by removing the jump terms associated with the half-chain subsystem from the full Liouvillian, we find that the long-time behavior with the anomalous tail of the half-chain WTD is governed by the eigenvalue $λ_0\:(<0)$ with the largest real part. We further reveal a qualitative change in the system-size dependence of $λ_0$ as a function of the measurement strength: for sufficiently weak measurement, $λ_0$ decreases proportionally to the system size, while for strong measurement, $λ_0$ scales independently of the system size, signaling the persistence of the anomalous half-chain WTD in the thermodynamic limit. The WTD is extracted solely from the spacetime record of quantum jumps $\{t_i,x_i\}$ and can be experimentally accessed without postselection. Our work establishes a spectral framework for understanding nontrivial WTDs in subsystems of monitored quantum dynamics and provides a novel diagnostics to assess many-body effects on WTDs.


---


## 结构检测显微镜

**Original Title:** Structured detection microscopy

**Authors:** Larnii Booth, Kyle Clunies-Ross, Rumelo Amor, Nicolas Mauranyapin, Zixin Huang, Michael A. Taylor, Warwick P. Bowen

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00413v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.00413v1

**Submitted:** 2026-04-01


### 摘要

超分辨率显微镜对于亚波长生物结构成像至关重要。然而，大多数技术依赖于发射器的非线性饱和或随机切换，限制了成像速度并增加了光毒性。在这里，我们在不使用饱和或随机动态学的情况下实现深度超分辨率，而是使用一种形式的空间模式解多路分解。通过塑造发射光的点扩展函数，我们的结构化检测显微镜（STM）将信息从图像的高散粒噪音区域重新分配，增强了对二维子散射发射器分离的敏感性，无需模式排序光学器件。在高数值口径全内反射荧光显微镜中实施STM，我们展示了附着在DNA纳米杆上的荧光团的成像，其间距小至50纳米，分辨率超过40纳米（比折射极限低五倍）。这表明空间模式解多路分解可以实现远亚波长分辨率，并且适用于生物相关样本。通过实现无发射极饱和和随机性的超分辨率生物分子成像，我们的工作为更好地理解生物结构、功能和动力学打开了大门。


### Abstract

Super-resolution microscopy is crucial for imaging sub-wavelength biological structures. However, most techniques rely on nonlinear saturation or stochastic switching of emitters, limiting imaging speed and increasing phototoxicity. Here, we achieve deep super-resolution without employing saturation or stochastic dynamics, instead using a form of spatial mode demultiplexing. By shaping the point-spread function of the emitted light, our Structured Detection Microscope (SDM) redistributes information away from high shot-noise regions of the image, enhancing sensitivity to sub-diffraction emitter separations in two-dimensions and without mode-sorting optics. Implementing SDM within a high-numerical aperture total internal reflection fluorescence microscope, we demonstrate imaging of fluorophores attached to DNA nanorulers with separations as small as 50 nm at resolutions surpassing 40 nm - fivefold below the diffraction limit. This shows that spatial mode demultiplexing can achieve far sub-wavelength resolution and is applicable to biologically relevant samples. By enabling super-resolution biomolecular imaging without emitter saturation and stochasticity, our work opens the door to better understanding biological structure, function and dynamics.


---


## 用位置和动量叠加描述非经典粒子的传播

**Original Title:** Characterization of non-classical particle propagation using superpositions of position and momentum

**Authors:** Yuki Senoo, Holger F. Hofmann, Hiroki Yamakami, Masataka Iinuma

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00417v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.00417v1

**Submitted:** 2026-04-01


### 摘要

不确定性原理提出了粒子传播中位置控制和动量控制之间的定量权衡。然而，具有截然不同不确定性权衡的两个状态的叠加引入了一个干涉项，该项似乎结合了关于位置和动量的精确陈述，使我们能够研究量子力学如何描述单个粒子在自由空间中的传播。在这里，我们对萨格纳克干涉仪中产生的位置和动量叠加中制备的量子进行了详细的实验研究。通过干涉仪输出端口处的三种不同测量设置获得了量子的横向分布，对应于初始位置分布、初始动量分布和初始位置和动量不确定度的贡献大致相等的中间传播时间。我们表明，干涉效应将量子定位在位置和动量的狭窄间隔中，导致随着干涉图案在中间位置展开，牛顿第一定律的定量违反。获得的数据可用于证明维格纳函数在位置和动量区间之外的区域中的负性，位置和动量贡献受到限制。


### Abstract

The uncertainty principle suggests a quantitative trade-off between the control of position and the control of momentum in particle propagation. However, a superposition of two states with very different uncertainty trade-offs introduces an interference term that seems to combine precise statements about position and about momentum, allowing us to study how quantum mechanics describes the propagation of individual particles in free space. Here, we present a detailed experimental study of photons prepared in a superposition of position and momentum generated in a Sagnac interferometer. The transverse distribution of photons was obtained with three different measurement settings at the output port of the interferometer, corresponding to the initial position distribution, the initial momentum distribution, and an intermediate propagation time at which the contributions of initial position and momentum uncertainties are approximately equal to each other. We show that the interference effect localizes the photons in narrow intervals of position and momentum, resulting in a quantitative violation of Newton's first law as the interference pattern spreads out at the intermediate position. The data obtained can be used to demonstrate the negativity of the Wigner function in regions outside the position and momentum intervals in which the position and momentum contributions are confined.


---


## 1-使用独立消散克尔孤立子实现200公里范围内的Mbps双场量子密钥分发

**Original Title:** 1-Mbps Twin-Field Quantum Key Distribution over 200 km Using Independent Dissipative Kerr Solitons

**Authors:** Hao Dong, Tian-Jiao Zhang, Yan-Wei Chen, Wei Sun, Cong Jiang, Sanli Huang, Shuyi Li, Di Ma, Xiang-Bin Wang, Yang Liu, Junqiu Liu, Qiang Zhang, Jian-Wei Pan

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00431v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.00431v1

**Submitted:** 2026-04-01


### 摘要

双场量子密钥分发（TF-QKD）通过其平方根扩展极大地提高了城市间距离的安全密钥速率（SKR）。通过并行QKD通道的时分多路传输（CDM）可以进一步提高总SKR。然而，TF-QKD中的直接实现带来了巨大的挑战，因为每个波长通道都需要独立的超稳定种子激光器、窄线宽度发射机和光闭环（OPLL），这些都不容易扩展。在这里，我们通过使用Alice和Bob的两个独立的集成消散克尔孤立子（DKS）微梳作为多波长源来规避这些限制。通过稳定每个梳状线的频率，可以实现所有波长通道上的高可见性单光子干涉-仅需要稳定两个微梳的泵浦波长和重复率。基于这种架构，我们使用发送或不发送协议进行了完整的TF-QKD实验，使用16个DWDM信道在201.1 km的光纤上实现了1.57 Mbps的总SKR。这一结果表明，在相同的距离下，与单波长TF-QKD相比，增强了一个数量级以上。考虑到单个DKS梳可以支持C波段上的100多条相干线，这种方法为跨城市距离的高速率量子密钥分发提供了一条可扩展的途径。


### Abstract

Twin-field quantum key distribution (TF-QKD) dramatically enhances the secure key rate (SKR) over inter-city distances through its square-root scaling. Further improvements in aggregate SKR can be achieved by wavelength-division multiplexing (WDM) of parallel QKD channels. However, direct implementation in TF-QKD poses significant challenges, as each wavelength channel requires an independent ultra-stable seed laser, narrow-linewidth transmitters, and optical phase-locked loops (OPLLs), which are not easily scalable. Here, we circumvent these limitations by employing two independent, integrated dissipative Kerr soliton (DKS) microcombs at Alice and Bob as multi-wavelength sources. High-visibility single-photon interference across all wavelength channels is achieved by stabilizing the frequencies of every comb line - requiring only the stabilization of the pump wavelength and repetition rates of the two microcombs. Based on this architecture, we perform a full TF-QKD experiment using the sending-or-not-sending protocol, achieving a total SKR of 1.57 Mbps over 201.1 km of fiber using 16 DWDM channels. This result represents more than an order-of-magnitude enhancement compared with single-wavelength TF-QKD at the same distance. Given that a single DKS comb can support over 100 coherent lines across the C-band, this approach offers a scalable pathway toward high-rate quantum key distribution over inter-city distances.


---


## 使用腔增强型SPDC源提高频率多路传输量子转发器中纠缠产生率

**Original Title:** Improvement of entanglement generation rate in frequency-multiplexed quantum repeaters using cavity-enhanced SPDC source

**Authors:** Ryoma Komatsudaira, Tomoyuki Horikiri

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00434v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.00434v1

**Submitted:** 2026-04-01


### 摘要

高速率纠缠产生对于实现实用量子转发器至关重要。为此，所使用的量子的频率多路传输是一种有效的方法。特别是，已经提出了使用腔增强自发参数下转换（cSPDC）作为光对源的方案。在这项研究中，为了对基于cSPDC的频率多路传输量子转发器进行理论性能评估，我们推导出频率多路传输的量子状态的近似表达，其中每个频率模式都被视为独立的双模式压缩真空（TMSV）状态。使用这个公式，我们计算了使用cSPDC频率多路传输的单量子干涉方案中几种情况下纠缠产生的预示概率和保真度。我们的结果表明，通过多路传输大约100种模式，对于基本链路距离$L_\mathrm{EL}=25 \mathrm{km}$，预示概率提高到大约98%，即使在所有模式的保真度超过0.9的情况下。此外，对于$L_\mathrm{EL}=100 \mathrm{km}$，我们表明，在保真度保持0.9或更高的情况下，预示概率（在单一模式情况下约为0.7%）增加到约38%。这些分析结果证明了使用cSPDC作为量子转发器的光对源的有效性。


### Abstract

High-rate entanglement generation is essential for the realization of practical quantum repeaters. To this end, frequency multiplexing of the photons employed is an effective approach. In particular, schemes using cavity-enhanced spontaneous parametric down-conversion (cSPDC) as a photon-pair source have been proposed. In this study, toward a theoretical performance evaluation of frequency-multiplexed quantum repeaters based on cSPDC, we derive an approximate expression for the quantum state of the frequency-multiplexed photons, where each frequency mode is treated as an independent two-mode squeezed vacuum (TMSV) state. Using this expression, we calculate the heralding probability and fidelity of entanglement generation for several cases in a single-photon interference scheme using frequency multiplexing with cSPDC. Our results demonstrate that by multiplexing approximately 100 modes, the heralding probability improves to approximately 98% for an elementary link distance $L_\mathrm{EL}=25 \mathrm{km}$, even in scenarios where the fidelity exceeds 0.9 across all modes. Furthermore, for $L_\mathrm{EL}=100 \mathrm{km}$, we show that the heralding probability, which was approximately 0.7% in the single-mode case, increases to about 38% under the condition that the fidelity remains 0.9 or higher. These analytical results demonstrate the effectiveness of employing cSPDC as a photon-pair source for quantum repeaters.


---


## 具有亚Prad相分辨率的抗噪纳米光电子陀螺仪

**Original Title:** Noise-resilient nanophotonic gyroscope with sub-prad phase resolution

**Authors:** Yu Tao, Xinhang Li, Jingzheng Huang, Zidi Lin, Yuyao Guo, Hongjing Li, Linjie Zhou, Guihua Zeng

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00459v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.00459v1

**Submitted:** 2026-04-01


### 摘要

基于Sagnac效应的光学陀螺仪是精确定位和导航的基石。然而，它们庞大的外形因素阻碍了在新兴的移动和自主系统中的部署。在纳米光子平台上，Sagnac信号在积极的小型化下直线下降。因此，信号很容易被折射率波动淹没，使导航级灵敏度在短短几平方毫米内成为一个众所周知的难以捉摸的目标。在这里，我们演示了一种抗噪纳米光陀螺仪，通过利用双链脱钩架构有效地将旋转信号与通道噪音隔离。该概念验证设备在3 mm 2无源硅氮芯片上实施，实现了1.42 °/h的偏置不稳定性和0.001 °/\squrt {h}的角度随机游走，分别比具有类似足迹的代表性纳米光电子陀螺仪提高了4个和6个数量级（参考文献27）。在集成光学陀螺仪的更广泛背景下，我们的方法将长期存在的尺寸性能差距缩小了两到三个数量级，将芯片级设备转移到以前无法达到的状态，并指向单片微系统的导航相关精度。该架构进一步实现了具有普遍适用性的亚普拉（sub-prad）阶段分辨率，为下一代稳健的、单片集成的光传感系统建立了基础框架。


### Abstract

Optical gyroscopes based on the Sagnac effect are the cornerstone of precision orientation and navigation. However, their bulky form factors prevent deployment in emerging mobile and autonomous systems. On nanophotonic platforms, the Sagnac signal plummets under aggressive miniaturization. Consequently, the signal is easily swamped by refractive-index fluctuations, rendering navigation-grade sensitivity within just a few square millimeters a notoriously elusive goal. Here, we demonstrate a noise-resilient nanophotonic optical gyroscope by exploiting a two-chain decoupling architecture to effectively isolate the rotation signal from channel noise. Implemented on a 3 mm^2 passive silicon nitride chip, the proof-of-concept device achieves a bias instability of 1.42 deg/h and an angle random walk of 0.001 deg/\sqrt{h}, representing improvements of 4 and 6 orders of magnitude, respectively, over the representative nanophotonic gyroscope of similar footprint (ref. 27). In the broader context of integrated optical gyroscopes, our approach bridges the long-standing size-performance gap by two to three orders of magnitude, moving chip-scale devices into a previously inaccessible regime and pointing toward navigation-relevant precision for monolithic microsystems. This architecture further enables sub-prad phase resolution with general applicability, establishing a foundational framework for the next generation of robust, monolithically integrated photonic sensing systems.

## 标准量子阶段估计通过随机初始状态检测所有特征值

**Original Title:** Standard Quantum Phase Estimation Detects All Eigenvalues via Randomized Initial States

**Authors:** Yuki Izumi, Hitoshi Kawahara

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00475v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.00475v1

**Submitted:** 2026-04-01


### 摘要

标准量子相估计（QPE）通常被认为不适合同时检测所有本征值，因为它需要初始状态与目标本征状态充分重叠。在本文中，我们表明这种限制并不是QPE电路本身固有的。标准QPE的输出分布可以写成Fejér核的叠加，该核由与本征模的平方重叠加权。我们证明，如果初始状态是在1-设计的每次激发时独立绘制的（特别是通过随机选择计算基本状态），则这些模式权重在期望值上均衡，从而产生状态平均QPE分布，该分布在每个特征相位置都表现出峰值。从这个意义上说，所有特征值都可以访问，而无需对标准QPE电路进行任何修改;重复的特征值通过其特征空间的总权重出现。对于满足分离条件的不同特征相，我们进一步建立了严格的峰值检测理论，并推导出用于检测所有峰值的充分射击计数估计。我们通过对计算机辅助工程（CAE）产生的1，008个自由度的有限单元法（Element）矩阵进行数值实验来验证该理论。


### Abstract

Standard quantum phase estimation (QPE) has often been regarded as unsuitable for simultaneous detection of all eigenvalues, because it requires initial states with sufficient overlap with the target eigenstates. In this paper, we show that this limitation is not inherent to the QPE circuit itself. The output distribution of standard QPE can be written as a superposition of Fejér kernels weighted by the squared overlaps with the eigenmodes. We prove that, if the initial state is independently drawn at each shot from a 1-design (in particular, by random selection of computational basis states), these mode weights are equalized in expectation, yielding a state-averaged QPE distribution that exhibits peaks at every eigenphase location. In this sense, all eigenvalues become accessible without any modification of the standard QPE circuit; repeated eigenvalues appear through the aggregated weight of their eigenspaces. For distinct eigenphases satisfying a separation condition, we further establish a rigorous peak-detection theory and derive a sufficient shot-count estimate for detecting all peaks. We validate the theory through numerical experiments on a finite element method (FEM) matrix with 1,008 degrees of freedom arising from computer-aided engineering (CAE).


---


## 液晶马约拉纳准粒子的编织和交换统计

**Original Title:** Braiding and exchange statistics of liquid crystalline Majorana quasiparticles

**Authors:** A. I. Tóth, G. Negro, A. D. Huxley, D. Marenduzzo

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00492v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.00492v1

**Submitted:** 2026-04-01


### 摘要

3D中的液晶缺陷可以被视为几何旋量，其出现的性质让人想起量子凝聚物质中的拓扑激发，例如马约拉纳准粒子。然而，目前尚不清楚这种类比有多深，也不清楚这是纯粹的数学映射，还是扩展到关键的物理特征，例如交换统计数据或编织行为。为了解决这个问题，我们在这里考虑一个由四个类似于June Majorana的缺陷轮廓组成的简单模式，并询问当我们将它们反复编织时，缺陷轮廓如何变化。令人惊讶的是，我们发现，在很大的参数空间中，缺陷轮廓的行为就像非阿贝尔任意子的经典类似物，在我们的情况下，这可以通过在类似布洛赫的半球上移动的缺陷双载体来描述。弹性相互作用和动力学效应增强了门的复杂性，门可以通过编织这些准粒子来实现，使这些液晶旋量有希望成为拓扑计算机组件的候选者。


### Abstract

Liquid crystalline defects in 3D can be viewed as geometric spinors, whose emergent properties are reminiscent of those of topological excitations in quantum condensed matter, such as Majorana quasiparticles. However, it is unclear how deep this analogy is, and whether this is a purely mathematical mapping, or it extends to key physical features, such as the exchange statistics or braiding behaviour. To address this question, here we consider a simple pattern made up of four nematic Majorana-like defect profiles, and ask how the defect profiles change as we braid them repeatedly around each other. Surprisingly, we find that in a large range of parameter space the defect profiles behave as classical analogues of non-Abelian anyons, which can be described in our case by defect bivectors moving on a Bloch-like hemisphere. Elastic interactions and dynamical effects enhance the complexity of the gates which can be performed by braiding these quasiparticles, making these liquid crystalline spinors promising candidates as components of topological computers.


---


## 量子安全代码审计：LLM辅助的静态分析和量子感知风险评分后量子密码迁移

**Original Title:** Quantum-Safe Code Auditing: LLM-Assisted Static Analysis and Quantum-Aware Risk Scoring for Post-Quantum Cryptography Migration

**Authors:** Animesh Shaw

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00560v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.00560v1

**Submitted:** 2026-04-01


### 摘要

加密相关量子计算机（CRQC）的即将到来威胁到现代软件的安全基础：Shor的算法破解了RSA、ECDSA、ECDH和迪夫-赫尔曼，而Grover的算法降低了对称和基于哈希的方案的有效安全性。尽管NIH于2024年标准化了后量子加密术（PQC）（TIP 203 ML-KEM、TIP 204 ML-DSA、TIP 205 SLH-DSA），但大多数代码库缺乏自动化工具来清点经典加密使用情况并根据量子风险优先考虑迁移。我们提出了量子安全代码审计器，这是一个量子感知的静态分析框架，它结合了（i）对15类量子脆弱基元的基于regex的检测，（ii）LLM辅助的上下文丰富来对使用情况和严重性进行分类，以及（iii）通过QisKit 2.x中实施的变分量子特征解算器（VQE）模型进行风险评分，结合量子比特成本估计来确定结果的优先顺序。我们在五个开源库（python-rsa、python-ecdsa、python-jose、node-jsonwebtoken和Bouncy Castle Java）中评估了该系统，涵盖了5，775个发现。在602个已标记实例的分层样本中，我们实现了71.98%的准确率、100%的召回率和83.71%的F1评分。所有代码、数据和复制脚本都以开源形式发布。


### Abstract

The impending arrival of cryptographically relevant quantum computers (CRQCs) threatens the security foundations of modern software: Shor's algorithm breaks RSA, ECDSA, ECDH, and Diffie-Hellman, while Grover's algorithm reduces the effective security of symmetric and hash-based schemes. Despite NIST standardising post-quantum cryptography (PQC) in 2024 (FIPS 203 ML-KEM, FIPS 204 ML-DSA, FIPS 205 SLH-DSA), most codebases lack automated tooling to inventory classical cryptographic usage and prioritise migration based on quantum risk. We present Quantum-Safe Code Auditor, a quantum-aware static analysis framework that combines (i) regex-based detection of 15 classes of quantum-vulnerable primitives, (ii) LLM-assisted contextual enrichment to classify usage and severity, and (iii) risk scoring via a Variational Quantum Eigensolver (VQE) model implemented in Qiskit 2.x, incorporating qubit-cost estimates to prioritise findings. We evaluate the system across five open-source libraries -- python-rsa, python-ecdsa, python-jose, node-jsonwebtoken, and Bouncy Castle Java -- covering 5,775 findings. On a stratified sample of 602 labelled instances, we achieve 71.98% precision, 100% recall, and an F1 score of 83.71%. All code, data, and reproduction scripts are released as open-source.


---


## 消散费米超流体的非平衡相转变：多端约瑟夫森结的案例研究

**Original Title:** Nonequilibrium phase transition of dissipative fermionic superfluids: Case study of multi-terminal Josephson junctions

**Authors:** Soma Takemori, Kazuki Yamamoto

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00574v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.00574v1

**Submitted:** 2026-04-01


### 摘要

我们研究了通过约瑟夫森结连接的费米子超流体三重体的非平衡动力学，在三种超流体之一的二体损失突然开启后。通过为Lindblad方程建立消耗性CSC理论，我们发现超流序参数表现出相旋转，从而产生对应于不同结的三种类型的直流约瑟夫森电流。我们证明，当没有二体损失的超流体之间的隧道幅度$V_{31}$较弱时，就会发生以直流约瑟夫森电流消失为特征的两步非平衡动态相转变（NDPT）：消散首先通过使一个直流约瑟夫森电流有限来诱导NDPT，而进一步增加的消散使剩余的直流约瑟夫森电流消失。相比之下，当$V_{31}$很强时，功耗会引发NDPT，其中所有直流约瑟夫森电流同时消失。基于简化模型的分析研究进一步支持了这一观察结果。


### Abstract

We investigate nonequilibrium dynamics of a triad of fermionic superfluids connected via Josephson junctions, following sudden switch-on of two-body loss in one of the three superfluids. By formulating the dissipative BCS theory for the Lindblad equation, we find that the superfluid order parameter exhibits a phase rotation, thereby giving rise to three types of dc Josephson currents corresponding to different junctions. We demonstrate that, when the tunneling amplitude $V_{31}$ between superfluids without two-body loss is weak, two-step nonequilibrium dynamical phase transition (NDPT) characterized by the vanishing dc Josephson currents occurs: dissipation first induces the NDPT by making one dc Josephson current finite, while further increasing dissipation makes this remaining dc Josephson current vanish. By contrast, when $V_{31}$ is strong, dissipation induces the NDPT in which all dc Josephson currents simultaneously vanish. An analytical study based on a simplified model further supports this observation.

## 拉盖尔-高斯态高能散射的普遍特征

**Original Title:** Universal features of high-energy scattering of Laguerre-Gaussian states

**Authors:** Yaoqi Yang, Igor P. Ivanov

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00575v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.00575v1

**Submitted:** 2026-04-01


### 摘要

量子、电子和其他粒子的涡旋状态是波包，携带固有轨道角动量（OSC），并表现出平面波无法实现的其他特征。一旦克服实验挑战，高能涡旋态的碰撞就可以成为核和粒子物理学的一个有前途的工具。关于涉及涡旋状态的散射过程存在大量文献;然而，大多数作品都依赖于在实验中难以实现的假设。在这项工作中，我们使用在非零影响参数$b$处碰撞的近轴拉盖尔高斯（LG）波包对涡旋状态散射过程进行了系统性的重新分析。由于总的最终横向动量$P_\perp$不再固定，因此我们重点关注差横截面积如何依赖于$P_\perp$。我们强调，非平凡的$P_\perp$-相关特征可以源自LG波包的形状，也可以源自感兴趣的散射过程的动力学。在这里，我们专注于前一个来源并详细探索这些普遍的运动学特征，而对特定过程的修改及其可能带来的新颖见解的研究则委托给未来的工作。有趣的是，非零影响参数$b$在许多$P_\perp$相关效应中发挥着关键作用，使其成为涡旋状态的有用探测器，而不是通常假设的干扰因素。


### Abstract

Vortex states of photons, electrons, and other particles are wave packets that carry intrinsic orbital angular momentum (OAM) and exhibit other features unavailable for plane waves. Collisions of high-energy vortex states can become a promising tool for nuclear and particle physics, once experimental challenges are overcome. An extensive literature exists on scattering processes involving vortex states; however, most works rely on assumptions that will be challenging to achieve in experiment. In this work, we initiate a systematic re-analysis of vortex-state scattering processes using paraxial Laguerre-Gaussian (LG) wave packets colliding at a non-zero impact parameter $b$. Since the total final transverse momentum $P_\perp$ is no longer fixed, we focus on how the differential cross section depends on $P_\perp$. We emphasize that non-trivial $P_\perp$-dependent features can originate either from the shape of the LG wave packets or from the dynamics of the scattering process under interest. Here, we focus on the former source and explore in detail these universal kinematic features, while the study of process-specific modifications, along with the novel insights they may bring, is delegated to a future work. Interestingly, the non-zero impact parameter $b$ plays a key role in many $P_\perp$-dependent effects, making it a useful probe of vortex states, not a nuisance factor as often assumed.


---


## 有理逼近的分数Poisson方程的量子算法

**Original Title:** Quantum algorithms for the fractional Poisson equation via rational approximation

**Authors:** Yin Yang, Yue Yu, Long Zhang, Ming Zhou

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00603v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.00603v1

**Submitted:** 2026-04-01


### 摘要

本文提出了一种求解有界区域上分数Poisson方程\（（-Δ）& s u = f\）的量子算法，其中\（s \in（0，1）\）。所提出的方法将理性逼近技术与量子线性系统求解器相结合，以实现指数级量子优势。有理逼近将逆分数拉普拉斯方程表示为标准解的加权和，将原始的非局部问题转化为一组移动整阶偏微方程。通过修改后的右侧结构，这些方程被合并到一个单一的大型线性系统中，该结构简化了量子实现。为了实现实际实施，我们通过薛定格化技术开发显式量子电路，该技术将线性系统的非正动力学转换为更高维度的薛定格型方程，允许使用标准的汉密尔顿模拟。电路结构利用位移运算符的分解来实现离散拉普拉斯，并采用受控操作来实现选择的Oracle。在有限差离散化下，我们利用系数矩阵的块编码技术提供了详细的算法过程。全面的复杂性分析表明，量子算法实现了对逆网格尺寸\（h &{-1}\）的依赖，该尺寸独立于空间维度\（d\），与在高维度中遭受指数增长的经典方法形成鲜明对比。这为多维分数问题建立了指数级量子优势，有效地克服了限制经典方法的维度诅咒。


### Abstract

This paper presents a quantum algorithm for solving the fractional Poisson equation \((-Δ)^s u = f\) with \(s \in (0,1)\) on bounded domains. The proposed approach combines rational approximation techniques with quantum linear system solvers to achieve exponential quantum advantage. The rational approximation represents the inverse fractional Laplacian as a weighted sum of standard resolvents, transforming the original nonlocal problem into a collection of shifted integer-order partial differential equations. These equations are consolidated into a single large linear system through a modified right-hand side construction that simplifies the quantum implementation. To enable practical implementation, we develop explicit quantum circuits via the Schrödingerization technique, which converts the non-unitary dynamics of the linear system into a higher-dimensional Schrödinger-type equation, allowing the use of standard Hamiltonian simulation. The circuit construction leverages the decomposition of shift operators to realize the discrete Laplacian and employs controlled operations to implement the select oracle. Under finite difference discretization, we provide detailed algorithmic procedures utilizing block-encoding techniques for the coefficient matrices. A comprehensive complexity analysis demonstrates that the quantum algorithm achieves a dependence on the inverse mesh size \(h^{-1}\) that is independent of the spatial dimension \(d\), in stark contrast to classical methods which suffer from exponential growth in high dimensions. This establishes an exponential quantum advantage for high-dimensional fractional problems, effectively overcoming the curse of dimensionality that limits classical approaches.


---


## 超越微扰理论：强关联多体系统的解析框架

**Original Title:** Beyond Perturbation Theory: A Resolvent-Based Framework for Strongly Correlated Many-Body Systems

**Authors:** Zhi-qiang Huang, Qing-yu Cai

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00606v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.00606v1

**Submitted:** 2026-04-01


### 摘要

基于局部分析性（泰勒展开）的传统微扰理论经常在能量间隙呈指数级小且相互作用强的多体系统中失败。这项工作提出了一种基于两个核心原则的替代方法论框架：（1）从分解物的极点展开开始，直接捕捉全局分析结构，（2）统计地处理局部波动（本着本征状态热化假说的精神）来关闭平均场方程。至关重要的是，我们通过推导互相关联项的精确回归重新展开来超越平均场水平，该重新展开系统性地生成控制分布尾部、分支分裂和波动的更高级修正。该框架是通过分层类比策略实现的，用洛伦兹、高斯和混合形式求解自相容方程，分别描述批量、尾部和完全分布。这种方法不依赖于弱耦合假设，适用于对不可积多体系统中的整体性质（例如，信息量）的定量分析。我们详细介绍了它的数学结构、波动的回归扩展、有效性条件、与传统方法的比较，并提供了通用的实现工作流程。


### Abstract

Traditional perturbation theory, based on local analyticity (Taylor expansion), often fails in many-body systems with exponentially small energy gaps and strong interactions. This work presents an alternative methodological framework built on two core principles: (1) starting from the pole expansion of the resolvent to directly capture the global analytic structure, and (2) treating local fluctuations statistically (in the spirit of the eigenstate thermalization hypothesis) to close the mean-field equations. Crucially, we go beyond the mean-field level by deriving an exact recursive re-expansion of the cross-correlated terms, which systematically generates higher-order corrections that control the distribution tails, branch splitting, and fluctuations. The framework is realized through a hierarchical ansatz strategy, solving self-consistent equations with Lorentzian, Gaussian, and hybrid forms to describe the bulk, tail, and full distribution, respectively. This methodology does not rely on weak-coupling assumptions and is applicable to the quantitative analysis of global properties such as entropy production and distribution functions in nonintegrable many-body systems. We detail its mathematical structure, the recursive expansion of fluctuations, conditions of validity, comparison with traditional methods, and provide a general implementation workflow.


---


## 没有量子优势意味着改进的边界和经典算法的二元油漆车间问题

**Original Title:** No quantum advantage implies improved bounds and classical algorithms for the binary paint shop problem

**Authors:** Mark Goh, Lara Caroline Pereira dos Santos, Matthias Sperl

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00607v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.00607v1

**Submitted:** 2026-04-01


### 摘要

二元喷漆车间问题（BPSP）是一个APX难优化问题，其中给定n个汽车模型在长度为2n的序列中出现两次，目标是找到一个着色序列，以便每个模型的两次出现的涂漆方式不同，同时最大限度地减少油漆沿着序列交换的次数。最近的经典启发式（称为循环星贪婪（RSG）算法）被假设为实现0.361的预期油漆交换比，从而优于电路深度p = 7的QAOA。由于具有对数电路深度的QAOA的性能与实例无关，因此平均油漆交换率受QAOA的上限，数字证据表明该比例大约在0.265和0.282之间。为了提供硬件相关的比较，我们还在D-Wave Quantum Annealer Advantage 2上实施了BPSP，获得了0.320的最低油漆交换比。鉴于具有log电路深度的QAOA对于BSPP等稀疏优化问题并不表现出量子优势，这意味着存在一种超越RSG算法和log深度QAOA的经典算法。我们提供了数字证据，证明平均场近似优化算法（MF-AOA）是一种这样的算法，它击败了迄今为止所有已知的经典启发式算法和量子算法，油漆交换率约为0.2799。


### Abstract

The binary paint shop problem (BPSP) is an APX-hard optimization problem in which, given n car models that occur twice in a sequence of length 2n, the goal is to find a colouring sequence such that the two occurrences of each model are painted differently, while minimizing the number of times the paint is swapped along the sequence. A recent classical heuristic, known as the recursive star greedy (RSG) algorithm, is conjectured to achieve an expected paint swap ratio of 0.361, thereby outperforming the QAOA with circuit depth p = 7. Since the performance of the QAOA with logarithmic circuit depth is instance independent, the average paint swap ratio is upper-bounded by the QAOA, which numerical evidence suggests is approximately between 0.265 and 0.282. To provide hardware-relevant comparisons, we additionally implement the BPSP on a D-Wave Quantum Annealer Advantage 2, obtaining a minimum paint swap ratio of 0.320. Given that the QAOA with logarithmic circuit depth does not exhibit quantum advantage for sparse optimization problems such as the BPSP, this implies the existence of a classical algorithm that surpasses both the RSG algorithm and logarithmic depth QAOA. We provide numerical evidence that the Mean-Field Approximate Optimization Algorithm (MF-AOA) is one such algorithm that beats all known classical heuristics and quantum algorithms to date with a paint swap ratio of approximately 0.2799.


---


## 洛伦兹破坏时空中非经典关联的生存

**Original Title:** Survival of nonclassical correlations in Lorentz-violating spacetime

**Authors:** Yangchun Tang, Zhilong Liu, Wentao Liu, Jieci Wang

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00616v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.00616v1

**Submitted:** 2026-04-01


### 摘要

洛伦兹不变性的崩溃，量子引力的一个潜在特征，提供了一个超越广义相对论的物理学窗口。我们研究了爱因斯坦-大黄蜂黑洞时空所体现的这种违反是如何影响非局域量子关联的。具体来说，我们研究了爱因斯坦-大黄蜂黑洞事件视界内外的量子转向和Bell非定域性。我们的分析表明，初始关联态的量子操纵被限制在事件视界附近的一个狭窄的区域，与洛伦兹破坏参数进一步限制这个域。值得注意的是，转向不对称程度受到距视界的距离和洛伦兹违规参数的显着调制，两个空间分离的区域表现出相反的趋势。此外，外部观察者可测量的贝尔非定域性随着与黑洞距离的增加而增强。这些发现证实了非经典相关性在违反洛伦兹的引力背景中的持续存在，并为量子信息和基本时空对称性之间的相互作用提供了一个新的视角。


### Abstract

The breakdown of Lorentz invariance, a potential signature of quantum gravity, offers a window into physics beyond general relativity. We investigate how such a violation, embodied by the Einstein-Bumblebee black hole spacetime, influences the nonlocal quantum correlations. Specifically, we study the quantum steering and Bell nonlocality between modes trapped inside and outside the event horizon of an Einstein-Bumblebee black hole. Our analysis demonstrates that quantum steering for an initially correlated state is confined to a narrow region near the event horizon, with the Lorentz-violating parameter further constraining this domain. Notably, the degree of steering asymmetry is significantly modulated by both the distance from the horizon and the Lorentz-violating parameter, with the two spatially separated regions exhibiting opposite trends. Furthermore, the Bell nonlocality measurable by an external observer strengthens with increasing distance from the black hole. These findings confirm the persistence of nonclassical correlations in a Lorentz-violating gravitational background and and offer a novel perspective on the interplay between quantum information and fundamental spacetime symmetries.


---


## 量子格子Boltzmann方法的量子机器学习：跨多个时间步非线性碰撞操作符的变分量子电路的可训练性

**Original Title:** Quantum machine learning for the quantum lattice Boltzmann method: Trainability of variational quantum circuits for the nonlinear collision operator across multiple time steps

**Authors:** Antonio David Bastida Zamora, Ljubomir Budinski, Pierre Sagaut, Valtteri Lahtinen

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00620v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.00620v1

**Submitted:** 2026-04-01


### 摘要

本研究探讨了量子机器学习（QML）在量子格子Boltzmann方法（QLBM）中逼近碰撞操作符的非线性分量的应用。为了实现这一目标，我们训练变分量子电路（VQC）来构造运算符$U$。当应用于线性碰撞后量子状态$\ket{_i}$时，该操作符产生最终状态$\ket{_f} = U\ket{_i}$，它成功复制了从Bhatnagar-Gross-Krook（BGK）逼近中推导出的非线性碰撞动力学。在这个框架中，我们提出了两种不同的架构：R1模型和R2模型。R1模型专为涉及多个时间步而无需中间测量的量子模拟而设计，重点是准确捕捉连续进化中的非线性动力学。相比之下，R2模型是为了用正运算符实现单个时间步的非线性运算符的高精度重建。


### Abstract

This study investigates the application of quantum machine learning (QML) to approximate the nonlinear component of the collision operator within the quantum lattice Boltzmann method (QLBM). To achieve this, we train a variational quantum circuit (VQC) to construct an operator $U$. When applied to the post-linear-collision quantum state $\ket{Ψ_i}$, this operator yields a final state $\ket{Ψ_f} = U\ket{Ψ_i}$ that successfully replicates the nonlinear collision dynamics derived from the Bhatnagar-Gross-Krook (BGK) approximation. Within this framework, we present two distinct architectures: the R1 model and the R2 model. The R1 model is designed for quantum simulations that involve multiple time steps without intermediate measurements, focusing on accurately capturing nonlinear dynamics in continuous evolution. In contrast, the R2 model is tailored to achieve the high-precision reconstruction of the nonlinear operator for a single time step with an unitary operator.


---


## 多量子位平台中局部激励生存概率的衰退

**Original Title:** Decay of the survival probability of a local excitation in multi-qubit platforms

**Authors:** Paolo Muratore-Ginanneschi, Bayan Karimi, Jukka Pekola

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00625v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.00625v1

**Submitted:** 2026-04-01


### 摘要

我们对最初在多量子位系统的单粒子部分准备的状态的生存概率进行了理论研究。我们工作的动机是正在实验室中不断开发基于超导体电路的多量子位平台。使用随机矩阵理论的基本概念，我们获得了平台数学模型中生存概率的分析表达，尽管这些模型已经被规范化，但之前已被证明可以为实验数据提供相关基准。特别是，我们表明，衰变性质对汉密尔顿运算符具有扩展状态的性质敏感。生存概率似乎并不取决于量子比特之间的相互作用是由高斯正交系综（通常被解释为“混沌”动力学模型）描述的，还是由解析可解链建模的。我们将这种现象解释为在纯粹的单一动力学中出现平衡的一般机制的表现。最后，在相同的假设下，一个初始的准备与投影上的一个大部分的扩展本征态的Hamilton算子，我们展示了如何扩展经典的Kac-Mazur-Montroll估计的返回时间的量子生存概率。


### Abstract

We present a theoretical study of the survival probability of a state initially prepared in the one-particle sector of a multi-qubit system. The motivation for our work is the ongoing laboratory development of multi-qubit platforms based on superconducting circuits. Using elementary concepts of random matrix theory, we obtain analytic expressions for the survival probability in mathematical models of platforms which, albeit stylized, have been previously shown to provide relevant benchmarks for experimental data. In particular, we show that the decay properties are sensitive to the property of the Hamilton operator to have extended states. The survival probability does not appear instead to depend on whether the interaction between qubits is described by a Gaussian orthogonal ensemble (often interpreted as a model of ''chaotic'' dynamics) or is modeled by an analytically solvable chain. We interpret this phenomenon as a manifestation of a general mechanism for the emergence of equilibration in purely unitary dynamics. Finally, under the same hypothesis of an initial preparation with projection on a large fraction of the extended eigenstates of the Hamilton operator, we show how to extend the classical Kac-Mazur-Montroll estimate of the return time to the quantum survival probability.


---


## 准周期格子中非线性诱导的无间隙抽运

**Original Title:** Nonlinearity-Induced Thouless Pumping in Quasiperiodic Lattices

**Authors:** Xiao-Xiao Hu, Dun Zhao, Hong-Gang Luo

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00639v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.00639v1

**Submitted:** 2026-04-01


### 摘要

非线性无激励抽运已经在周期格子中建立了;其在准周期格子中的对应抽运尚未被探索。在这里，我们展示了准周期格子中间隙孤波的非线性拓扑，其中局部非线性自相容势导致格子势重建;因此，由这种局部重建引发的新兴拓扑结构控制着间隙孤波的动力学。这使得孤立子能够以物理方式占据单个的拓扑带，实现准量子化无拉曼抽运。此外，本征格子微扰扰乱了这种能带占据，从而驱使孤立子进入非量子化漂移区。然而，即使在这个区域中，我们也发现孤立子输运也受到临界有理逼近的拓扑性质的限制。调整非线性或网格缩放揭示了拓扑抽运、漂移和局部化之间的可控切换。我们的工作揭示了复杂格子势中非线性诱导的拓扑行为的机制。


### Abstract

Nonlinear Thouless pumping has been established in periodic lattices; its counterpart in quasiperiodic lattices remains unexplored. Here, we show a nonlinear topological pumping of gap solitons in quasiperiodic lattices where the local nonlinear self-consistent potentials lead to a lattice potential reconstruction; as a result, an emergent topological structure induced by this local reconstruction governs the dynamics of the gap solitons. This enables solitons to adiabatically occupy a single topological band, realizing quasi-quantized Thouless pumping. In addition, the intrinsic lattice perturbations disrupt this band occupation, which drives solitons into a non-quantized drifting regime. However, even in this regime, we also find that the soliton transport is constrained by the topological properties of a critical rational approximant. Tuning nonlinearity or lattice scaling reveals a controllable switching among topological pumping, drifting, and localization. Our work uncovers a mechanism for nonlinearity-induced topological behavior in complex lattice potentials.


---


## 非log凹重尾分布Gibbs期望的量子算法

**Original Title:** Quantum Algorithms for Gibbs Expectation of Non-log-concave and Heavy-tailed Distributions

**Authors:** Xinmiao Li, Jin-Peng Liu

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00656v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.00656v1

**Submitted:** 2026-04-01


### 摘要

我们为经典吉布斯期望建立了一个无偏量子采样和估计协议的系统框架。该框架推广了现有的配分函数估计方法，并在各个领域具有更广泛的应用。我们考虑在强凸性之外的宽松假设（例如消散性）下对一类广泛的非log-凹分布（尤其是重尾分布）进行抽样和估计。   我们开发了量子加速多层蒙特卡罗（QA-MLMC）的无偏扩展，以消除离散化和时间截断的所有偏差，并通过Radon-Nikodym求导引入测量变化方法和Girsanov定理。因此，我们的方法在误差$e $内实现了量子复杂性$\widetilde{\mathCal{O}}（e ^{-1}）$，而经典MLMC需要$\widetilde{\mathCal{O}（e ^{-2}）$，而现有的量子算法在更强的假设下产生有偏估计。此外，我们的统一框架能够在转换后对某些重尾分布进行无偏量子采样和估计。我们提供了我们的方法在统计、机器学习和金融领域的几种具体应用，以应对随机过程量子加速的更实际场景。


### Abstract

We establish a systematic framework of unbiased quantum sampling and estimation protocols for the classical Gibbs expectation. This framework generalizes existing approaches to the partition function estimation and has broader applications in various fields. We consider sampling and estimation for a wide class of non-log-concave distributions, particularly heavy-tailed ones, under relaxed assumptions beyond strong convexity, such as dissipativity.
  We develop an unbiased extension of quantum-accelerated multilevel Monte Carlo (QA-MLMC) to eliminate all biases from discretization and time truncation, together with introducing a change-of-measure approach and the Girsanov theorem via Radon-Nikodym derivatives. As a result, our approach achieves quantum complexity $\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-1})$ within error $ε$, whereas the classical MLMC requires $\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-2})$ and existing quantum algorithms yield biased estimators under stronger assumptions. Furthermore, our unified framework enables unbiased quantum sampling and estimation for certain heavy-tailed distributions after transformation. We provide several concrete applications of our approach in statistics, machine learning, and finance, towards more practical scenarios of the quantum acceleration of stochastic processes.


---


## 在开放量子动力学中学习隐藏结构

**Original Title:** Learning Hidden Structures in Open Quantum Dynamics

**Authors:** Alexander Teretenkov, Sergey Kuznetsov, Alexander Pechen

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00711v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.00711v1

**Submitted:** 2026-04-01


### 摘要

我们引入了一种机器学习方法，用于在受限制的实验访问下识别开放量子动力学的隐藏结构特征。与大多数现有的专注于检测或预测动态行为的数据驱动方法不同，我们的框架的目标是有效马尔科夫进化背后的不变代数结构的推断。测量限制、对称性和超选择规则通过可访问的可观察量的$*$-代数描述合并。学习问题被表述为来自多次测量序列的最大似然估计，其中不变子代数的代数类型--明确地说是无去相关子代数--被视为离散结构假设。该方法的可行性在多个合成模型和一个导量子电动力学系统上得到了说明，其中直接从测量数据中识别出非平凡的中间代数结构。


### Abstract

We introduce a machine-learning approach for identifying hidden structural features of open quantum dynamics under restricted experimental access. Unlike most existing data-driven methods which focus on detection or prediction of dynamical behavior, our framework targets the inference of invariant algebraic structures underlying the effective Markovian evolution. Measurement limitations, symmetries, and superselection rules are incorporated through a $*$-algebraic description of accessible observables. The learning problem is formulated as maximum-likelihood estimation from multi-time measurement sequences, where the algebraic type of an invariant subalgebra - articularly a decoherence-free subalgebra - is treated as a discrete structural hypothesis. The feasibility of the approach is illustrated on multiple synthetic models and a waveguide quantum electrodynamics system, where nontrivial intermediate algebraic structures are identified directly from measurement data.


---


## 约束失配引起的可调信息绝缘

**Original Title:** Tunable information insulation induced by constraint mismatch

**Authors:** Akshay Panda, Anwesha Chattopadhyay

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00732v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.00732v1

**Submitted:** 2026-04-01


### 摘要

我们研究了两个具有双重约束的$1D$ $PXP$链的复合模型，形成了一个接头，充当量子信息交换的无限运动学障碍。此外，可以通过放松连接部位的约束来使连接处的硬壁成为可渗透的，防止复合链两侧之间的任何量子信息泄漏。多个冻结的结将Hilbert空间破碎成不相交的Krylov碎片，其数量随着工程缺陷的增加而呈指数级增加。此外，每个量子分解扇形中的能量水平统计是严格的Poissonian，这表明不相交的Hamilton的张量和会导致子$PXP$链的混乱谱的纯叠加。我们还发现可能存在一种手征保护的零能量模式，该模式在物理边缘和结点附近的体内具有局部峰值。这种状态受到保护，不会与任何手征保留障碍引起的体状态杂交。由于本征函数的张量积结构，非零能量疤痕状态的数量也成倍增加。最后，我们引入了具有空间可调热区和无热区的新型Fock态。这种架构可以使用光钳、定址束和促进技术在可编程里德伯原子平台中轻松实现。


### Abstract

We study a composite model of two $1D$ $PXP$ chains with dual constraints, forming a junction that acts as an infinite kinematic barrier to quantum information exchange. Moreover, the hard wall at the junction which acts as a perfect reflector, preventing any quantum information leakage between the two sides of the composite chain, can be made permeable by relaxing the constraint at the junction sites. Multiple frozen junctions shatter the Hilbert space into disjoint Krylov fragments, the number of which increases exponentially with the engineered defects. Furthermore, the energy level statistics in each symmetry-resolved sector are strictly Poissonian, demonstrating that the tensor sum of the disjoint Hamiltonians results in a pure superposition of the chaotic spectra of the sub- $PXP$ chains. We also find that a chirally protected zero-energy mode can exist which has local peaks at the physical edges and within the bulk near the junction sites. This state is protected from hybridization with bulk states induced by any chirality preserving disorder. Due to the tensor product structure of the eigenfunctions, the non-zero energy scar states also multiply in number. Finally, we introduce novel Fock states with spatially tunable thermal and athermal regions. This architecture can be readily realized in programmable Rydberg atom platforms using optical tweezers, addressing beams and facilitation techniques.


---


## 为实时安全应用程序设计基于相噪的量子随机数生成器：设计、验证和可扩展性

**Original Title:** Engineering a Phase-Noise-Based Quantum Random Number Generator for Real-Time Secure Applications: Design, Validation, and Scalability

**Authors:** Anurag K. S. V., Shubham Chouhan, K. Srinivasan, G. Raghavan, Kanaka Raju P

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00741v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.00741v1

**Submitted:** 2026-04-01


### 摘要

随机数发生器（RNG）对于从密码学到模拟等应用至关重要。根据随机性的来源，RNG分为伪随机数生成器（PRNG）、真随机数生成器（TRNG）和量子随机数生成器（QRNG）。这项工作提出了高速、高效、基于相噪的QRNG系统的端到端开发，该系统利用单频激光器的量子相噪，随机性源于自发发射。使用在阈值附近工作的半导体激光器（线宽$\大约$5.23 $GHz$）和$\sim$48 $厘米$光纤延迟线进行自差测量，获得了2.0 $Gbps$的原始数据生成率。为了确保QRNG输出的均匀随机性，使用了内部开发的稳健提取技术，例如Toeplitz Strong Extractor（PSE）。使用NIH和Diehard测试套件进行随机性验证，确认所有统计测试均在标准置信水平下通过。开发的系统在运行中实现了1.0 $Gbps$的后处理生成率，技术就绪级别（TRL）为7，接近TRL 8，适合密钥生成和随机建模等实时安全应用。


### Abstract

Random Number Generators (RNGs) are crucial for applications ranging from cryptography to simulations. Depending on the source of randomness, RNGs are classified into Pseudo-Random Number Generators (PRNGs), True Random Number Generators (TRNGs), and Quantum Random Number Generators (QRNGs). This work presents the end-to-end development of a high-speed, high-efficiency, phase-noise-based QRNG system that taps into the quantum phase noise of a single-frequency laser, with randomness originating from spontaneous emission. Using a self-heterodyne measurement with a semiconductor laser (linewidth $\approx$ 5.23 $GHz$) operated near threshold and a $\sim$48 $cm$ fiber delay line, a raw data generation rate of 2.0 $Gbps$ is achieved. To ensure uniform randomness in the QRNG output, robust extraction techniques developed in-house, such as the Toeplitz Strong Extractor (TSE), are used. Randomness validation using the NIST and Diehard test suites confirms that all statistical tests pass at standard confidence levels. The developed system achieves a post-processed generation rate of 1.0 $Gbps$ in operation and attains a Technology Readiness Level (TRL) of 7, approaching TRL 8, making it suitable for real-time secure applications such as cryptographic key generation and stochastic modeling.


---


## 探索分子合成维度中的拓扑边状态

**Original Title:** Probing topological edge states in a molecular synthetic dimension

**Authors:** Adarsh P. Raghuram, Francesca M. Blondell, Jonathan M. Mortlock, Benjamin P. Maddox, Sohail Dasgupta, Holly A. J. Middleton-Spencer, Kaden R. A. Hazzard, Hannah M. Price, Philip D. Gregory, Simon L. Cornish

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00745v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.00745v1

**Submitted:** 2026-04-01


### 摘要

工程合成维度（在量子系统的内部状态内模拟额外空间维度的物理学）允许实现实验中无法实现的现象。超冷接地状态极分子是编码合成维度的理想平台，可以访问与旋转和超精细自由度相关的长寿命内状态的大型Hilbert空间，这些内状态可以与微波场耦合在一起以模拟隧道效应。在这里，为了对超冷分子的优势进行基准测试，我们在超冷RbCs分子的旋转状态中编码了一个1D合成格子，并使用它来研究著名的Su-Schrieffer-Heeger（SSH）模型，这是一个显示出拓扑性质的最小模型。为了探测该系统，我们使用辅助旋转状态进行光谱学，并研究确定性状态准备后的时间动态。我们证明了很长的相干时间，通常是格子隧道周期的~500倍，即使对于使用8个旋转状态的合成格子也是如此。长时间观察动力学并对合成维度进行完全现场分辨读出，使我们能够测试手征和非手征微扰对被保护的边缘状态的影响。我们的工作为使用分子丰富的内部结构进行进一步的量子模拟奠定了基础，包括相互作用的分子样本中的偶极弦相，以及多体Hamilton的隔热状态准备。


### Abstract

Engineering synthetic dimensions, where the physics of additional spatial dimensions is simulated within the internal states of a quantum system, allows the realisation of phenomena not otherwise accessible in experiments. Ultracold ground-state polar molecules are an ideal platform to encode synthetic dimensions, offering access to large Hilbert spaces of long-lived internal states associated with the rotational and hyperfine degrees of freedom, that can be coupled together with microwave fields to simulate tunnelling. Here, to benchmark the advantages of ultracold molecules, we encode a 1D synthetic lattice in the rotational states of ultracold RbCs molecules and use it to investigate the well-known Su-Schrieffer-Heeger (SSH) model, a minimal model displaying topological properties. To probe the system, we perform spectroscopy using an auxiliary rotational state and study the time dynamics after deterministic state preparation. We demonstrate long coherence times, typically ~500 times the lattice tunnelling period, even for a synthetic lattice using 8 rotational states. Observations of dynamics at long times with full site-resolved readout of the synthetic dimension allow us to test the effects of chiral and non-chiral perturbations on the topologically protected edge states. Our work lays the foundation for further quantum simulations using the rich internal structure of molecules, including dipolar string phases in interacting samples of molecules, and adiabatic state preparation of many-body Hamiltonians.


---


## 一致状态等级的下限

**Original Title:** Lower Bounds on Coherent State Rank

**Authors:** Florian Cottier, Ulysse Chabaud

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00766v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.00766v1

**Submitted:** 2026-04-01


### 摘要

大约相干状态等级是逼近连续变量玻色子量子状态所需的（经典）相干状态的最小数量，并且直接与模拟玻色子计算的经典复杂性相关。尽管它很重要，但人们对这个数量的下限知之甚少，即使对于基本的州家庭也是如此。在这项工作中，我们开始了对近似连贯状态阶下限的系统研究。我们的贡献如下。   (i)我们引入了一种基于低阶逼近理论的技术，该技术产生了任意单一模式状态的近似相干状态阶的通用下限。   (ii)使用这种技术，我们找到了有限近似相干态阶的所有单一模式状态的完整描述，并且我们特别获得了压缩态和有限叠加Fock态的近似相干态阶的解析表达。   (iii)我们进一步表明，对于多模式Fock状态的有限叠加，我们的单模式下限可以提升到多模式下限。   (iv)最后，我们证明了$n$-模Fock状态$的近似相干状态阶的超多项下界|1\rangle #{\otimes n}$，通过利用与永久的连接。为此，我们证明了永久值的近似多线性公式的代数复杂性是超多项的，其基础是[Raz，JASM 2009]对精确公式的下限的证明。   我们的结果为通过相干状态分解对玻色子采样进行高效经典模拟建立了无条件的障碍，并将玻色子量子系统的非经典性与代数复杂性中的中心问题联系起来。


### Abstract

The approximate coherent state rank is the minimal number of (classical) coherent states required to approximate a continuous-variable bosonic quantum state and directly relates to the classical complexity of simulating bosonic computations. Despite its importance, little is known about lower bounds on this quantity, even for basic families of states. In this work, we initiate a systematic study of lower bounds on the approximate coherent state rank. Our contributions are as follows.
  (i) We introduce a technique based on low-rank approximation theory yielding generic lower bounds on the approximate coherent state rank of arbitrary single-mode states.
  (ii) Using this technique, we find a complete characterization of all single-mode states of finite approximate coherent state rank, and we obtain in particular analytical expressions for the approximate coherent state rank of squeezed states and of finite superpositions of Fock states.
  (iii) We further show that our single-mode lower bounds can be lifted to multimode lower bounds for finite superpositions of multimode Fock states.
  (iv) Finally, we prove a super-polynomial lower bound on the approximate coherent state rank of the $n$-mode Fock state $|1\rangle^{\otimes n}$, by exploiting a connection to the permanent. To do so, we show that the algebraic complexity of approximate multi-linear formulas for the permanent is super-polynomial, building upon the proof of a lower bound for exact formulas due to [Raz, JACM 2009].
  Our results establish an unconditional barrier to efficient classical simulation of Boson Sampling via coherent state decompositions and connect non-classicality of bosonic quantum systems to central questions in algebraic complexity.


---


## 激光中的振动诱发共振

**Original Title:** Vibrationally Induced Resonances in Lasing

**Authors:** Kai Müller, Kimmo Luoma, Christian Schäfer

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00798v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2604.00798v1

**Submitted:** 2026-04-01


### 摘要

光学电路和光源（例如激光器）经历了不断的小型化。在极端情况下，纳米激光器可能仅由限制在等离子体纳米共振器中的少数分子组成。少发射器激光器承诺低能量需求和快速响应，可插入任何设备或生物组织。利用最近开发的堆叠层次方法，根据第一原则，我们以等离子体激元腔中的少分子激光为例，证明了振动结构对激光的影响。明确解释整个振动多管齐下，揭示了激光强度的共振，该共振取决于斯托克斯频移、驱动强度和发射器数量。我们的工作确定了无处不在的“非连贯驱动”--逼近的局限性，并为理解分子规模的纳米激光器铺平了道路。


### Abstract

Optical circuits and light sources, such as lasers, undergo continuous miniaturization. In its extreme, nanolasers might be comprised of only a few molecules confined in plasmonic nanoresonators. Few-emitter lasers promise low energy requirements and fast responses in a footprint that can be inserted into any device or biological tissue. Utilizing the recently developed stacked hierarchy approach, informed from first principles, we demonstrate the impact of vibrational structure on lasing, using the example of few-molecule lasing in plasmonic cavities. Explicitly accounting for the entire vibrational manifold unveils resonances in the laser intensity that depend on the Stokes shift, drive strength, and the number of emitters. Our work identifies the limits of the omnipresent "incoherent drive"-approximation and paves the way for the understanding of nanolasers at the molecular scale.
